SHA-256 hash duplicate detector

This hash detector matched the BYTES not the filenames because I had multiple that had the filename.0.laz and all types of stuff. 

//////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

The other one that I made was 

$seen = @{}
Get-ChildItem -Filter *.laz | ForEach-Object {
    if ($seen.ContainsKey($_.Name)) {
        Write-Host "Duplicate found â†’ deleting $($_.FullName)"
        Remove-Item $_.FullName -Force
    } else {
        $seen[$_.Name] = $true
    }
}

which just detects filename duplicates. 

//////////////////////////////////////////////

Below is a log  of running the script. I accidentally deleted the Duplicate found from each of these because I thought it might not have worked and was going to turn the detected duplicates into a .CSV and try something else.
However it correctly ID'd and deleted over 3000 files.

Loading personal and system profiles took 2024ms.
(base) PS C:\Users\epoc8> cd Z:\1LIDAR\RAW\CA_SierraNevada_4_2022
$hashTable = @{}
Get-ChildItem -Filter *.laz | ForEach-Object {
    $hash = (Get-FileHash $_.FullName -Algorithm SHA256).Hash
    if ($hashTable.ContainsKey($hash)) {
        Write-Host "$($_.FullName) matches $($hashTable[$hash])"
        Remove-Item $_.FullName -Force
    } else {
        $hashTable[$hash] = $_.FullName
    }
}
